record(bi, "$(PREFIX)FFO:01:ClearFault_RBV") {
  field(DESC, "Might be overidden by PLC writes")
  field(SCAN, "I/O Intr")
  field(PINI, "1")
  field(TSE, "-2")
  field(DTYP, "asynInt32")
  field(INP, "@asyn($(PORT),0,1)ADSPORT=851/POLL_RATE=1/GVL.g_FastFaultOutput1.i_xReset?")
  field(ZNAM, "FALSE")
  field(ONAM, "TRUE")
  info(archive, "VAL")
}
